              <a role="menuitem" class="js-selected-navigation-item dropdown-item" data-selected-links=" /sbatrow?tab=sponsoring" href="/sbatrow?tab=sponsoring" data-turbo-frame="user-profile-frame">Sponsoring</a>
            </li>
        </ul>
      </details-menu>
</div>
</details></details-toggle>
